 1237 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | * Create_Sprite — Compiled sprite engine

 1240 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 1241 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 1242 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *
 1243 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 1244 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 1245 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *
 1246 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
 1247 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written
 1248 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     13 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $04 ADRL Shape_Adr   — input: shape pixel data (24-bit)
 1249 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     14 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $08 ADRL Msk_Adr     — $000000=none, $FFFF00=auto, $FEFE00=decor

 1251 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     16 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $0E DA   Nb_Lgn      — bytes per shape row
 1252 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     17 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $10 DA   Nb_Col      — bytes per shape column
 1253 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     18 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $12 DA   Lgn         — row ($FFFF=dynamic via Y register)
 1254 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     19 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0880               | *   $14 DA   Col         — column
